Because O

is O
a O

. O

silver-grey O

. O

( O

. O

) O

the O

of O

of O

COOKIES O

Materials O

As O

. O

. O

Using O
Teak O

Teak O
is O
a O
close O
grained O
hardwood O
with O
a O
high O
natural O
oil O
content O
. O

This O
makes O
it O
hard O
wearing O
, O
highly O
resistant O
to O
rotting O
and O
almost O
impervious O
to O
the O
effects O
of O
sun O
, O
rain O
, O
frost O
or O
snow O
. O

These O
characteristics O
combine O
to O
make O
it O
the O
ideal O
timber O
for O
all O
outdoor O
applications O
. O

Only O
premium O
grade O
plantation-grown O
teak O
is O
used O
for O
the O
manufacture O
of O
Gloster O
furniture O
. O

features O
of O
premium O
grade O
teak O
are O
a O
straight O
grain O
structure O
, O
the O
absence O
of O
knots O
, O

or O

and O
an O
even O
overall O
colour O
. O
